#cheat Real Time Clock
//ID: 12043
//Score: 125
//Author: vettefan88
//Category: Misc
//Description: This will make the game time move in real time.
//what this means is that a minute in real life will be a minute in the game.
//
//So if you synchronize the times when you start playing, The time will remain consistent with real time.
//Image: none
//Time: 02/06/2006 19:34:16
//Working: Yes
setint(0x08B5E08C, 60000);
#off
setint(0x08B5E08C, 1000);
